###  Vieno‚ÇÅ

This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Vieno* (FIXME)
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  1
* Origin:  finer|joukahainen
* Possible NER class:  FIRST
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
* Semantic tags:  FEMALE
